< text>
Highly recommended! My husband and I went out on the queen of hearts on a rock cod trip. It was my first fishing trip. I was impressed! Eric was our guide, helper, untangler, janitor (they were very organized for a safe COVID experience) and fish filleter! He made sure we all had a great time and it was clear the guest experience was a great priority. We saw loads of whales, sunfish, jellyfish all day - Plus we caught our full bag limit with some beautiful big fish so that made it even better!

We will be coming back to try our hand at Salmon. Thank you guys!</text>

< review>
Mcgrath has a great reputation and I don't doubt their staff's ability to care for the animals, but my only experience with them made me realize they were not a good fit for us.
Generally, I think it's tough taking a cat to a clinic with dogs, especially when a drop off is required due to the pandemic, so the odds weren't in our favor going in.
The vet I spoke to over the phone was kind and took time to hear me out when I described my cat's worrying behaviors, but seemed busy and told me that she thinks my cat is 4-5 years older than I believed (he was a rescue, so we don't know for sure) which was pretty shocking news. I wish we could have discussed that more, and that I had gotten a little more counseling on the medication they prescribed, especially because they were much more expensive than the cats-only vet I normally use.
When I brought my cat home, he was shaking for the rest of the day (I'm guessing because he was scared of the dogs in the facility). I had never seen him so scared, even when we first brought him home from the rescue. My cat's lasting anxiety after the visit meant we wouldn't return, but all of that said, I do think they would be a great vet for dogs.< /review>

I visited 4 different Veterinarians in the last 8 months and did not like any of them. They were either arrogant, inexperienced, insensitive, or gone out of the exam room in 60 seconds. I was getting really discouraged! Then a friend told me about McGrath Veterinary.

< Review>
Dr. McGrath is absolutely THE BEST VET in this entire area!  He is kind, caring, thorough and extremely knowledgeable.  I am a savvy and sophisticated consumer when it comes to medicine both for my family and my pets, and there is no vet who tops Brian McGrath in so many ways.

I have been going to Dr. McGrath for over a decade, following him through 2 other vet centers and now to his own in Sherman Oaks.  I am not a ‚Äúschlepper‚Äù but getting my dog the best care possible means going to Dr. McGrath---and driving from Pacific Palisades to the valley as I pass  many other veterinarians along the way.

Brian McGrath graduated from the top vet school on the East Coast, and is smart and wise when it comes to diagnostics and treatment.  He is also an outstanding surgeon.  I went to a W.L.A. animal hospital several years back and asked the staff who their best surgeon was (out of a couple dozen doctors that worked there) and they recommended Dr. McGrath.  The surgery went flawlessly and Dr. McGrath was so conscientious at follow-up afterwards.

Compassionate is an understatement when referring to Dr. McGrath.  He came in to his closed office on his day off when my beloved dog was dying.  He talked with me and helped me understand why putting him to sleep was truly the best option.   I could not have had anyone better---with his huge and caring heart, to be with me but Dr. McGrath at that difficult time.

And, if this was not enough for an outstanding vet, there is one more thing:  his prices.  Dr. McGrath is extremely fair in all of his charges.  He does not recommend additional treatments that jack up bills but may be unnecessary.  His skill and the amount of time he spends doing thorough exams are first rate, but his charges for such high-quality treatment are not.  The old adage: ‚Äúyou pay for what you get‚Äù does not apply when it comes to Dr. McGrath.

Go to this happily married father of four---and son who grew up inspired by his father, also a veterinarian, and you will be as devoted a follower of Dr. McGrath as I have been for past last dozen years.< /Review>

<rating>2<//rating>< text>
It is ho-hum Chinese food. Ordered lunch special with Kung-Pao chicken, which included soup, eggroll & soft drink. I wanted hot-n-sour soup. It was neither hot nor sour. The vegetables in it were extremely under-cooked and it was not even hot, temperature wise. Egg roll was a spring roll with vegetables nearly raw inside. Ordered a diet Coke to drink and realized it tasted more like club soda than a Coke. Kung-Pao  chichken I know is a spicy dish. Their version is NOT. And I am not sure if it is because it is the lunch special but, I had to look for chicken pieces in the mush they served under this name. Fried rice was okay but not much fried with anything. 2 pieces of eggs I was able to find in a pint size bowl of fried rice. I don't believe I will be a regular customer of this joint, even though it is one of the very few places within walking distance from my work.< /text>

<review>This is my second time here. The first time i was completely blown away at how perfectly Ray and Sandys Hideaway fit the profile of a dive bar. As me and my date read reviews of the bar while sitting at the bar, we could not hold in our outbursts of laughter.
I ordered a bottle of coors lite and my date ordered a shot of Jager ( totaled less than $10) as my date took shot after shot, so did our petite and beautiful Bartender.
You basically need scuba gear because this a deep sea dive bar. There is no security ( unless you count the tiny female bartender or regular custys that might jump in to stop fights)
The kitchen is located directly in the bar( btw the bartender is also the cook)
The best part is the Decor! As you walk in you see outdated beer promotions all over the walls which are wood on one side and brick on the other. The owner has a very "tasteful" velvet nude painting of herself that favors the classic Jesus with Thorns paintings you can find in most pisa grandma houses along with their plastic covered couches located next to the Bitchen (Bar and Kitchen)
The ceiling tiles are artistic with what i assume to be personal peices of art work from regular customers. Consider it the dive bar Sistine Chapel.
I could go on and on but i conclude with giving this bar 5 stars. If you want to get drunk, sing and hear bad kareoke in your pajamas this is the place to go. I Love It. <text>FIRST TIME EATER!

Went on a work lunch with 2 other amazing ladies to Sushi Yama today - first time ever going here even though its literally walking distance from my office. However I will TOTALLY be back.

We had amazing service from Amber. She was super attentive and nice, quick, efficient and catered to any request we had.

The food was AMAZING! I eat pretty healthy and so I am always aware that I could easily eat 15 sushi rolls and be stoked about it but I need to be strategic.

Their menu is online and was available for me to check out prior to arriving. I knew exactly what I wanted and it came out even better than I anticipated.

I am not sure why I haven't been there before but it will definitely be a return.

It was so delicious I literally just asked my husband if he wanted to go tonight on a date night!

5 out of 5 would definitely recommend!

- Masks to and from tables
- Casual environment
- Will be an epic summer eatery as they keep it really cold in their due to food that they serve (I recommend a jacket if you run cold)
- No outside smokers air comes in
- Split tab friendly
- Great service
- Very reasonably priced
- Indoor and patio seating

< review>
Very nice sushi restaurant in Escondido. Appreciated the service the most but the food was good and they offered 50% off rolls. We started with the Pan Fried Gyozs which is basically dumplings with sesame ponzu which came out fast and was so good!!

For rolls we got a bunch and they were all good!!! We got the (1) Escondido (my favorite) which was shrimp tempura, crab, cucumber, tuna, salmon, eel, avo, topped with spicy aioli, eel sauce, & potato crunches; (2) The Centipede which was shrimp tempura, spicy tuna, cucumber, topped with avocado & balsamic glaze; (3) Orange County which was spicy crab, cucumber, topped with salmon, avocado, and yuzu essence, and finally a standard crunchy roll which was shrimp tempura, crab, cucumber, tempura flakes and soy glaze

If I had any complaint it would be that the rolls weren't rolled very well so they fall apart big time but the taste, service, and reasonable price will get me to go back there<//review>

Service was not very good. Parking is bad. Portions are huge. It tastes pretty good. Not very traditional, or made traditionally. I sat at the counter.  If you are looking for someone with the traditional 7 years sushi rice training, this is not the place. I really doubt it. The gentleman use plastic wrap to shape their sushi roles. They forgot one of our roles and served it a good 20 minutes after we finished our others. I asked for my check when food was delivered. took another 10 minutes to give it to me AFTER we finished eating. We were going to the theater afterwards. I dinno. If you are a teenager or a drunk person and want a fun place to hang, cool. The atmosphere was cool. It has value. My 16 year son thought it was good. He enjoyed himself.</Review>
